<aside
class="bio">









<p
class="title">about</p>









<p
class="bio">
Aerosmith
were
one
of
the
most
popular
hard
rock
bands
of
the
'70s,
setting
the
style
and
sound
of
hard
rock
and
heavy
metal
for
the
next
two
decades
with
their
raunchy,
bluesy
swagger.
The
Boston-based
quintet
found
the
middle
ground
between
the
men...
</p>









<a
href="/aerosmith/bio">read
more</a>








</aside>
